####### THE DWARVES OF MIDDLE EARTH #######				
				
### In order: 				
#	
## Longbeards			
# Line of Durin
# line of Delingur "keepers of thorin's halls"
# Line of Wegdrasil. Longbeard inhabitants of Tumnogoth Iaur
# Line of uni. "merchants of the river lhun. Guardians of the river waystation of Kheledul"
# Line of Hor "Longbeard colonists of the northern blue mountains"
# Line of Gorin (Nordinbad) "Guardians of Azan-zaram"
## Firebeards
# Line of Uri "lineofuri"
# Line of Khathzâ ibriz "khathzaibriz"
# Line of Ubraz. Guardians of the golden gate and stewards of Amak Arazi
# House of Arsan. Venerable, dying house of firebeards in the southern regions of Buzra Dum
# House of Agzay. Humble isolationists
# Line of Stone-Wall. Stalwart defenders of the gate of fire, and friends to all who come in peace
# Line of Hersar. Able captains of the Bronze guard
## Broadbeams
# Line of Dwalin
# Line of Gemkarsh

#####################################				
##### The Line of Durin ####				
#####################################
